<p>Borrowed from  a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source. 
Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bashkir_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bashkir language">Bashkir</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ba">ҡалпаҡ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ba-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qalpaq</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">калфак</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qalfaq</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazakh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kazakh language">Kazakh</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kk">қалпақ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qalpaq</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uzbek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Uzbek language">Uzbek</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="uz">qalpoq</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">kalpak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cap</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колпак.html>колпа́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kolpák</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колпак.html>колпака́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колпак.html>колпаки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колпак.html>колпако́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Russian-high-crowned_cap">high-crowned cap: cook cap, kalpak, fool's cap, nightcap etc.

***колпачок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:колпачок.html>колпачо́к</a> (16111)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колпак.html>колпа́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolpák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колпачок.html>колпачо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kolpačók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колпачок.html>колпачка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колпачок.html>колпачки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колпачок.html>колпачко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колпак.html>колпа́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolpák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: small high-crowned cap: cook cap, kalpak, fool's cap, nightcap, etc.</li>
<li>cap, curfew, capsule, hood</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> diaphragm <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">contraceptive</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

***колыхать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:колыхать.html>колыха́ть</a> (23952)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колыхать.html>колыха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kolyxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">колыхну́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rhythmically sway, to rock gently</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to excite, to emotionally move</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колыхать.html>колыха́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolyxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колыхаться.html>колыха́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kolyxátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колыхнуться.html>колыхну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to heave, to sway, to wave, to flutter <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of flags</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to flicker <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a flame</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колыхать.html>колыха́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolyxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колыхнуться.html>колыхну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kolyxnútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колыхаться.html>колыха́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to heave, to sway, to wave, to flutter (of flags)</li>
<li>to flicker (of a flame)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">колыхну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolyxnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***кольнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кольнуть.html>кольну́ть</a> (15291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кольнуть.html>кольну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kolʹnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>коло́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to prick, to sting</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have a stitch, to feel a prick or a stab
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:кольнуть.html>кольну́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лев.html>ле́вом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>боку́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>kolʹnúlo</b> v lévom bokú.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>felt a prick</b> in my left side.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***кольцевой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кольцевой.html>кольцево́й</a> (13176)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кольцо.html>кольцо́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolʹcó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ево́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кольцевой.html>кольцево́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kolʹcevój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>annular</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ring; circular
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кольцевой.html>кольцево́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kolʹcevóje</b> dvižénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>circular</b> motion</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кольцевой.html>кольцева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́га</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kolʹcevája</b> doróga</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>ring/circular/belt</b> road; orbital motorway</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кольцевой.html>кольцево́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:маршрут.html>маршру́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kolʹcevój</b> maršrút</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>circular</b> route</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кольцевой.html>кольцева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:церемония.html>церемо́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kolʹcevája</b> ceremónija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>ring</b> ceremony</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***кольцо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кольцо.html>кольцо́</a> (1852)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the same root as <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колесо.html>колесо́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kolesó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кольцо.html>кольцо́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kolʹcó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кольцо.html>кольца́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кольцо.html>ко́льца</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кольцо.html>коле́ц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ring</li>
<li>hoop</li>
<li>webring</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> roundabout (a road junction at which traffic streams circularly around a central island)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>коло́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ю́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-júčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li>thorny, spiny, prickly

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> biting, cutting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:колючий.html>колю́чий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>koljúčij</b> jazýk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sharp tongue</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>ком</a> (7908)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>ком</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kom</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ком.html>ко́ма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ком.html>ко́мья</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ком.html>ко́мьев</a><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* The plural noun forms are non-standard.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>

<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:блин.html>блин</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всегда.html>всегда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ком.html>ко́мом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pérvyj blin vsegdá kómom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you must spoil before you spin, practice makes perfect</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">first pancake is always a blob</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нда</a> (773)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">commande</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kommando</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нда</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kománda</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нды</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нд</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>command, order</li>
<li>team, crew, party</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> detachment</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crew, ship's company</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> team</li></ol>

<ol><li>—</li>

***командировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:командировать.html>командирова́ть</a> (15794)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed around 1600 from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kommandieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">commander</i>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нда</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kománda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ирова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-irovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:командировать.html>командирова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">komandirovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to send on an official/business trip, to send on a mission [an assignment]</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:командированный.html>командиро́ванный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">komandiróvannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:командировка.html>командиро́вка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">komandiróvka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:командировочный.html>командиро́вочный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">komandiróvočnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:командировочный.html>командиро́вочные</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">komandiróvočnyje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нда</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kománda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
